***выпятить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выпятить.html>вы́пятить</a> (12202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пя́тить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjátitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпятить.html>вы́пятить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výpjatitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпячивать.html>выпя́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick out, to thrust out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выпятить.html>вы́пятить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грудь.html>грудь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výpjatitʹ</b> grudʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw out one's chest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to over-emphasize, to over-stress</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выпячивать.html>выпя́чивать</a> (20690)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпятить.html>вы́пятить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výpjatitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпячивать.html>выпя́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vypjáčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпятить.html>вы́пятить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick out, to thrust out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выпячивать.html>выпя́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грудь.html>грудь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vypjáčivatʹ</b> grudʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw out one's chest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to over-emphasize, to over-stress</li></ol>

***вырабатывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырабатывать.html>выраба́тывать</a> (11586)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выработать.html>вы́работать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrabotatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырабатывать.html>выраба́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyrabátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выработать.html>вы́работать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to manufacture, to produce, to make
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырабатывать.html>выраба́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:электроэнергия.html>электроэне́ргию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyrabátyvatʹ</b> elektroenɛ́rgiju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to generate electricity</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to work out, to draw up, to elaborate</li>
<li>to form, to cultivate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырабатывать.html>выраба́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyrabátyvatʹ</b> v sebé silu vóli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cultivate a strong will</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make, to earn</li>
<li>to use up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырабатывать.html>выраба́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:топливо.html>то́плива</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyrabátyvatʹ</b> zapás tópliva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to burn up fuel</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mining</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырабатывать.html>выраба́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скважина.html>сква́жину</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyrabátyvatʹ</b> skvážinu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to work out a well</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырабатываться.html>выраба́тываться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vyrabátyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выработаться.html>вы́работаться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výrabotatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырабатывающий.html>выраба́тывающий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyrabátyvajuščij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выработать.html>вы́работать</a> (8077)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vy-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выработать.html>вы́работать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrabotatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырабатывать.html>выраба́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make, to manufacture, to produce</li>
<li>to cultivate, to develop, to form <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">including certain qualities pertaining to a person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выработать.html>вы́работать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:характер.html>хара́ктер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výrabotatʹ</b> xarákter</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to develop</b> a character</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выработать.html>вы́работать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:терпение.html>терпе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výrabotatʹ</b> v sebé terpénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to develop</b> patience in oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выработать.html>вы́работать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обаяние.html>обая́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výrabotatʹ</b> obajánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to develop</b> charm</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to exhaust, to use up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">by using something to extreme or until it is not functional</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выравнивание.html>выра́внивание</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyrávnivanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выравнивание.html>выра́внивания</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выравнивание.html>выра́внивания</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выравнивание.html>выра́вниваний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>smoothing, levelling</li>
<li>alignment, equalization</li>
<li>justification <i>(of a text)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выравнивать.html>выра́внивать</a> (28144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выровнять.html>вы́ровнять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrovnjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выравнивать.html>выра́внивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyrávnivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выровнять.html>вы́ровнять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to (make) even, to smooth out, to make level</li>
<li>to flatten (out)</li>
<li>to iron out (differences)</li>
<li>to align, to line up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to adjust or form to a line</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выравнивать.html>выра́внивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:край.html>кра́ю</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyrávnivatʹ</b> po právomu kráju</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to right-<b>align</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to equalize</li>
<li>to justify (e.g. text on a page)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выражаться.html>выража́ться</a> (3418)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выражать.html>выража́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выражаться.html>выража́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyražátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выразиться.html>вы́разиться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to express oneself</li>
<li>to manifest oneself</li>
<li>to swear, to use bad / strong language</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выражать.html>выража́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выражаться.html>выража́ясь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mjáxko <b>vyražájasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put it mildly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выразиться.html>вы́разиться</a> (4581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выразить.html>вы́разить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrazitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выразиться.html>вы́разиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrazitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выражаться.html>выража́ться</a></b>)
</p>

<li>to manifest oneself</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырасти.html>вы́расти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrasti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vy-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>расти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырасти.html>вы́расти</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrasti</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>расти́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырастать.html>выраста́ть</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растить.html>расти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырастить.html>вы́растить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrastitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выращивать.html>выра́щивать</a></b>)
